openvas-libraries-doc in Fedora 34

This page displays detailed information for a specific version of openvas-libraries-doc. You might want go back to the main page of openvas-libraries-doc.

Changelog

Date Author Change
2020-05-23 josef radinger - 11.0.1-1 - bump version - fix path to Source1 - add Buildrequires on libxml2-devel
2020-01-29 Fedora Release Engineering - 11.0.0-3 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_32_Mass_Rebuild
2020-01-17 Jeff Law - 11.0.0-2 - Change misguided strncpy calls into strcpy calls to avoid (proper) gcc diagnostic about length of strncpy call being the same as the source string length
2019-10-15 Michal Ambroz - 11.0.0-1 - bump to gvm-libs version 11.0.0 - put back the signature checking
2019-07-25 Fedora Release Engineering - 10.0.0-2 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_31_Mass_Rebuild

2019-02-26 josef radinger - 9.0.3-6 - make doc-full - better description for doc-sub-package
2019-02-03 josef radinger - 9.0.3-5 - add BuildRequires on graphviz
2019-02-02 josef radinger - 9.0.3-4 - enable net-snmp-devel - add openvas-libraries-snmp.patch (snmp -> netsnmp) - add openvas-libraries-gcc-warnings.patch to silence compiler warning - small reordering in spec-file - add openvas-libraries-buffer.patch - disable stringop-truncation on fedora >= 30
2019-02-01 Fedora Release Engineering - 9.0.3-3 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_30_Mass_Rebuild
